Our camp site was located ca. 45 minute walk from the end of the road to the south bank of the Rio San Jose. The camp was in virtually untouched primary forest and we eventually had trails on the other side of the river that allowed access to primary, foothill forest. See field notes (deposited at Univ. of Kansas Biodiversity Institute) for more details and hand drawn map of the area. Most bird species had finished breeding (apparently late March-early May) as most were in the final stages of the molt cycle. Very little was vocalizing, even at dawn. The following list is a compilation of species recorded, 4-28 July 1990. See daily lists for specifics. Does not include birds recorded that I did not see or hear.
